***отстреливать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отстреливать.html>отстре́ливать</a> (32260)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отстрелить.html>отстрели́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otstrelítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отстреливать.html>отстре́ливать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otstrélivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отстрелить.html>отстрели́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to shoot off (a body part)</li>
<li>to cause to forcibly separate, to eject, to jettison</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отстреливаться.html>отстре́ливаться</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otstrélivatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">отстрели́ться</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otstrelítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">отстреля́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otstreljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отстреливать.html>отстре́ливать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otstrélivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">отстреля́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">hunting</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to kill by shooting</li>
<li>to shoot (a predetermined amount of ammunition)</li></ol>

***отстрелить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отстрелить.html>отстрели́ть</a> (29010)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-стрели́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-strelítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отстрелить.html>отстрели́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otstrelítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отстреливать.html>отстре́ливать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to shoot off (a body part)</li>
<li>to selectively shoot (some members of a group)</li>
<li>to cause to forcibly separate, to eject, to jettison</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>стре<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ля́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>

***отступать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отступать.html>отступа́ть</a> (3569)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ступать.html>ступа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stupátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отступать.html>отступа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otstupátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отступить.html>отступи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to retreat, to fall back</li>
<li>to digress, to back off</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отступиться.html>отступи́ться</a> (13703)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отступить.html>отступи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otstupítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отступиться.html>отступи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otstupítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">отступа́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to give up, to renounce

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-сыла́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sylátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отсылать.html>отсыла́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otsylátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отослать.html>отосла́ть</a></b>)

<ol><li>to send away, to send off, to dispatch</li>
<li>to send back</li>
<li>to refer <i>(to)</i>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>сы́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:пан.html>пан</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:отсыпать.html>отсыпа́ть</a> (26988)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">от-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпать.html>сы́пать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sýpatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отсыпать.html>отсы́пать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otsýpatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:отсыпать.html>отсыпа́ть</a></strong></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">the impf./pf. forms differ in the word stress in the infinitive and the conjugation</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>to pour off, to separate by pouring out (bulk material, objects or pieces, not liquid)</li>
<li>to pour out <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">thereby reducing the quantity; bulk material, objects or pieces, not liquid</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to give generously</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отсыпаться.html>отсы́паться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otsýpatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:отсыпаться.html>отсыпа́ться</a></strong></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">the impf./pf. forms differ in the word stress in the infinitive and the conjugation</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отсыпаться.html>отсыпа́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">otsypátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:отсыпаться.html>отсы́паться</a></strong></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">the impf./pf. forms differ in the word stress in the infinitive and the conjugation</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pour out, to spill out <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a small quantity of a bulk material, objects, or pieces, not liquid</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>сы<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>па́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:отоспаться.html>отоспа́ться</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>от-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-сып-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b>.

***оттаивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оттаивать.html>отта́ивать</a> (25462)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оттаять.html>отта́ять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ottájatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оттаивать.html>отта́ивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ottáivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оттаять.html>отта́ять</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to thaw out, to let thaw out <i>(transitive)</i></li>
<li>to thaw out <i>(intransitive)</i></li>
<li>to thaw <i>(out)</i>, to melt, to mellow, to relax</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:таять.html>та́ять</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">tájatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:растаять.html>раста́ять</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rastájatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">та́яние</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">tájanije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>та́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:оттаять.html>отта́ять</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>от-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-та-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ива</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>
